                  </form>, as though it were pl. of <foreign lang="ar">تَبْشِيرٌ</foreign>, inf. n. of <foreign lang="ar">بَشَّرَ</foreign>; (A;) a word which has not its like except in the instances of <foreign lang="ar">تَعَاشِيبُ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">تَعَاجِيبُ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">تَفَاطِيرُ</foreign> [and <foreign lang="ar">تَبَاكِيرُ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">تَبَارِيحُ</foreign>, and probably a few others]; (TA;) <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">Annunciations; foretokens; foretellers; foreshowers; prognostics; earnests;</hi> of what is good:] the <hi rend="ital">beginnings</hi> of anything: (S, K:) the <hi rend="ital">first</hi> of blossoms &amp;c.: (TA:) the <hi rend="ital">beginnings,</hi> (S, K,) or <hi rend="ital">first annunciations,</hi> (A,) of daybreak; (S, A, K;) as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n2609-1" target="بَشَائِرُ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>: (TA:) it has no verb: (S:) and [is said to have] no sing.: but in a trad. of El-Hajjáj, <foreign lang="ar">تَبْشِيرٌ</foreign> occurs as meaning <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  the <hi rend="ital">commencement</hi> of rain. (TA.) One says, <foreign lang="ar">فِيهِ مَخَايِلُ</foreign>
